           <div> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>I have a document that was made in jsoup that looks like this</p> 
             <pre><code>Document doc = Jsoup.connect("http://en.wikipedia.org/").get();
</code></pre> 
             <p>How do i convert that <code>doc</code> into a string.</p>

         <h2> 3 Answers <span style="display:none;" itemprop="answerCount">3</span> </h2> 
         <div> 
          <div id="tabs"> 
           <a href="/questions/6865090/how-do-i-convert-a-document-made-in-jsoup-the-java-html-parser-into-a-string?answertab=active#tab-top" title="Answers with the latest activity first">active</a>

           <a class="youarehere" href="/questions/6865090/how-do-i-convert-a-document-made-in-jsoup-the-java-html-parser-into-a-string?answertab=votes#tab-top" title="Answers with the highest score first">votes</a>

       <a name="6865134"></a> 
       <div id="answer-6865134" class="answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="6865134" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer" itemprop="acceptedAnswer"> 
        <table> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td class="votecell"> 
            <div class="vote"> 
             <input type="hidden" name="_id_" value="6865134"> 
             <a class="vote-up-off" title="This answer is useful">up vote</a> 
             <span itemprop="upvoteCount" class="vote-count-post ">11</span> 
             <a class="vote-down-off" title="This answer is not useful">down vote</a> 
             <span class="vote-accepted-on load-accepted-answer-date" title="loading when this answer was accepted...">accepted</span> 
            </div> </td> 
           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>Have you tried:</p> 
             <pre><code>Document doc = Jsoup.connect("http://en.wikipedia.org/").get();
String htmlString = doc.toString();
</code></pre> 
             <p>As <em>Document</em> extends <em>Element</em> it also has got the method <em>html()</em> which "Retrieves the element's inner HTML" according to the <a href="http://jsoup.org/apidocs/">API</a>. So that should work:</p> 
             <pre><code>Document doc = Jsoup.connect("http://en.wikipedia.org/").get();
String htmlString = doc.html();
</code></pre> 
             <p><strong>Additional Info:</strong></p> 
             <p>Each <em>Document</em> object has got a reference to an instance of the inner class <em>Document.OutputSettings</em> which can be accessed via the method <em>outputSettings()</em> of Document. There you can enable/disable pretty-printing by using the setter <em>prettyPrint(true/false)</em>. See the API for <em>Document</em> and <em>Document.OutputSettings</em> for furtherinformation</p> 
            </div>

       <a name="25635651"></a> 
       <div id="answer-25635651" class="answer" data-answerid="25635651" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer"> 
        <table> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td class="votecell"> 
            <div class="vote"> 
             <input type="hidden" name="_id_" value="25635651"> 
             <a class="vote-up-off" title="This answer is useful">up vote</a> 
             <span itemprop="upvoteCount" class="vote-count-post ">0</span> 
             <a class="vote-down-off" title="This answer is not useful">down vote</a> 
            </div> </td> 
           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <ol> 
              <li>Elements post = d.select("div.post-content");</li> 
              <li>String dd = post.toString();</li> 
              <li>Document ddd = Jsoup.parse(dd);</li> 
             </ol> 
             <p>After parsing the string to document then you can use on it document functions</p> 
             <ol> 
              <li>Elements scriptTag = ddd.getElementsByTag("script");</li> 
              <li>System.out.println(scriptTag);</li> 
             </ol> 
            </div>

        $('#herobox li').click(function () {
            StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
                StackExchange.gps.track("aboutpage.click", { aboutclick_location: "hero" }, true);
            });

            window.location.href = '/tour';
        });
        $('#tell-me-more').click(function () {
            StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
                StackExchange.gps.track("aboutpage.click", { aboutclick_location: "hero" }, true);
            });
        });
        $('#herobox #close').click(function () {
            StackExchange.using("gps", function () {
                StackExchange.gps.track("hero.action", { hero_action_type: "minimize" }, true);
            });
            $.cookie("hero", "mini", { path: "/", expires: 365 });
            $.ajax({
                url: "/hero-mini",
                success: function (data) {
                    $("#herobox").fadeOut("fast", function () {
                        $("#herobox").replaceWith(data);
                        $("#herobox-mini").fadeIn("fast");
                    });
                }
            });
            return false;
        });
    </script>

      <h1 itemprop="name"><a href="/questions/6865090/how-do-i-convert-a-document-made-in-jsoup-the-java-html-parser-into-a-string" class="question-hyperlink">How do I convert a document made in Jsoup (the Java html parser) into a string</a></h1> 
     </div> 
     <div id="mainbar"> 
      <div class="question" data-questionid="6865090" id="question"> 
       <script>

           <div> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>I have a document that was made in jsoup that looks like this</p> 
             <pre><code>Document doc = Jsoup.connect("http://en.wikipedia.org/").get();
</code></pre> 
             <p>How do i convert that <code>doc</code> into a string.</p>

         <h2> 3 Answers <span style="display:none;" itemprop="answerCount">3</span> </h2>

          <div id="tabs"> 
           <a href="/questions/6865090/how-do-i-convert-a-document-made-in-jsoup-the-java-html-parser-into-a-string?answertab=active#tab-top" title="Answers with the latest activity first">active</a>

       <a name="6865134"></a> 
       <div id="answer-6865134" class="answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="6865134" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer" itemprop="acceptedAnswer"> 
        <table> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td class="votecell"> 
            <div class="vote"> 
             <input type="hidden" name="_id_" value="6865134"> 
             <a class="vote-up-off" title="This answer is useful">up vote</a> 
             <span itemprop="upvoteCount" class="vote-count-post ">11</span> 
             <a class="vote-down-off" title="This answer is not useful">down vote</a> 
             <span class="vote-accepted-on load-accepted-answer-date" title="loading when this answer was accepted...">accepted</span> 
            </div> </td> 
           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>Have you tried:</p> 
             <pre><code>Document doc = Jsoup.connect("http://en.wikipedia.org/").get();
String htmlString = doc.toString();
</code></pre> 
             <p>As <em>Document</em> extends <em>Element</em> it also has got the method <em>html()</em> which "Retrieves the element's inner HTML" according to the <a href="http://jsoup.org/apidocs/">API</a>. So that should work:</p> 
             <pre><code>Document doc = Jsoup.connect("http://en.wikipedia.org/").get();
String htmlString = doc.html();
</code></pre> 
             <p><strong>Additional Info:</strong></p> 
             <p>Each <em>Document</em> object has got a reference to an instance of the inner class <em>Document.OutputSettings</em> which can be accessed via the method <em>outputSettings()</em> of Document. There you can enable/disable pretty-printing by using the setter <em>prettyPrint(true/false)</em>. See the API for <em>Document</em> and <em>Document.OutputSettings</em> for furtherinformation</p> 
            </div>

       <a name="25635651"></a> 
       <div id="answer-25635651" class="answer" data-answerid="25635651" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer"> 
        <table> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td class="votecell"> 
            <div class="vote"> 
             <input type="hidden" name="_id_" value="25635651"> 
             <a class="vote-up-off" title="This answer is useful">up vote</a> 
             <span itemprop="upvoteCount" class="vote-count-post ">0</span> 
             <a class="vote-down-off" title="This answer is not useful">down vote</a> 
            </div> </td> 
           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <ol> 
              <li>Elements post = d.select("div.post-content");</li> 
              <li>String dd = post.toString();</li> 
              <li>Document ddd = Jsoup.parse(dd);</li> 
             </ol> 
             <p>After parsing the string to document then you can use on it document functions</p> 
             <ol> 
              <li>Elements scriptTag = ddd.getElementsByTag("script");</li> 
              <li>System.out.println(scriptTag);</li> 
             </ol> 
            </div>

        function createEditor() {

                postfix: "",

                    discardSelector: ".discard-answer"
                ,immediatelyShowMarkdownHelp:true
                });
                

        }
    });

     <div id="question-header"> 
      <h1 itemprop="name"><a href="/questions/6547033/update-text-in-html-page-using-parser" class="question-hyperlink">update text in HTML page using parser</a></h1> 
     </div> 
     <div id="mainbar"> 
      <div class="question" data-questionid="6547033" id="question"> 
       <script>

          <td class="postcell"> 
           <div> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>I always gets error in the <code>middlebitparent.replaceWith(nodespan);</code> in the following code which is written in jsoup to navigate the HTML doc and change the background color of word "In"</p> 
             <pre><code>Elements divs= doc.select("div");
          for(Element div : divs)
          {
               if (div.hasText())
                {
                    int pos = div.text().indexOf("In");
                    out.println(pos);
                    if (pos &gt;= 0)
                        {
                        Element span = doc.createElement("span");
                        span.attr("style", "background-color: yellow");
                        TextNode text = new TextNode(div.text(),"");
                      //  String[] words = div.split("\\s", 4);
                     TextNode middlebit = text.splitText(4);
                     TextNode endbit=text.splitText("In".length());           
                      Node middleclone = middlebit.clone();
                      span.appendChild(middleclone);
                      Node nodespan=span.clone();
                      Node middlebitparent = middlebit.parent();
                      middlebitparent.replaceWith(nodespan);
</code></pre> 
             <p>The error says </p> 
             <pre><code>java.lang.NullPointerException
    org.apache.jsp.Page1_jsp._jspService(Page1_jsp.java:177)
    org.apache.jasper.runtime.HttpJspBase.service(HttpJspBase.java:70)
    javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet.service(HttpServlet.java:717)
    org.apache.jasper.servlet.JspServletWrapper.service(JspServletWrapper.java:374)
    org.apache.jasper.servlet.JspServlet.serviceJspFile(JspServlet.java:342)
    org.apache.jasper.servlet.JspServlet.service(JspServlet.java:267)
    javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet.service(HttpServlet.java:717)
</code></pre> 
             <h2>UPDATE:</h2> 
             <p>Is there any parser which can update text in text node in an easy way</p>

       <a name="6555841"></a> 
       <div id="answer-6555841" class="answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="6555841" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer" itemprop="acceptedAnswer"> 
        <table> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td class="votecell"> 
            <div class="vote"> 
             <input type="hidden" name="_id_" value="6555841"> 
             <a class="vote-up-off" title="This answer is useful">up vote</a> 
             <span itemprop="upvoteCount" class="vote-count-post ">0</span> 
             <a class="vote-down-off" title="This answer is not useful">down vote</a> 
             <span class="vote-accepted-on load-accepted-answer-date" title="loading when this answer was accepted...">accepted</span> 
            </div> </td> 
           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <pre><code>    public static void main(String[] arg){
         HtmlCleaner cleaner = new HtmlCleaner();
         try {
             TagNode nodes = cleaner.clean(new File("c:/test.xml"));
             Object[] objects = nodes.evaluateXPath("//div/a[text(.,'In')]");
             System.out.println(((TagNode)objects[0]).getText());
         } catch (Exception e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }
</code></pre> 
             <p>You can try HtmlCleaner which support XPath which will be more useful in your case. Jsoup's CSS selector cannot filter the text node.</p>

      <h1 itemprop="name"><a href="/questions/10915493/getjson-jquery-illegalstateexception" class="question-hyperlink">$.getJSON JQuery - IllegalStateException</a></h1>

          <td class="postcell"> 
           <div> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>could someone please help me out? I am using JQuery $.getJSON() to load the contents of one dropdown (subcategories) based on the the selected dropdown (category).</p> 
             <p>I am getting an IllegalStateException for some reason. Thank you ahead of time.</p> 
             <pre><code>&lt;script&gt;
    $(document)
            .ready(
                    function() {

                        // reload subcategories when changing category
                        $('#categories').change(loadSubcategories);

                    });

    // load the subcategories based on selected category
    function loadSubcategories() {
        $.getJSON('findSubcategoriesForCategory.html', {
            categoryId : $('#categories').val(),
            ajax : 'true'
        }, function(data) {
            var html = '&lt;option value=""&gt;Select Subcategory&lt;/option&gt;';
            var len = data.length;
            for ( var i = 0; i &lt; len; i++) {
                html += '&lt;option value="' + data[i].id + '"&gt;' + data[i].name
                        + '&lt;/option&gt;';
            }
            html += '&lt;/option&gt;';

            $('#subcategories').html(html);

        });
    }
&lt;/script&gt;
</code></pre> 
             <p>Here is the code for the Controller method:</p> 
             <pre><code>@RequestMapping(value = "findSubcategoriesForCategory", method = RequestMethod.GET)
public @ResponseBody
List&lt;Subcategory&gt; findSubcategoriesForCategory(
        @RequestParam(value = "categoryId", required = true) String categoryId) {

    List&lt;Subcategory&gt; returnList = new ArrayList&lt;Subcategory&gt;();

    try {
        returnList = categoryService
                .findSubcategoriesForCategory(categoryId);
    } catch (Exception e) {
        LOGGER.error("An Error occured when Finding sub-categories for category id: " + categoryId);
    }

    return returnList;

}
</code></pre>

            // Have to fire editor after snippets, if snippets enabled

                ,immediatelyShowMarkdownHelp:true
                });
                

        }
    });

    <title type="text">How do I convert a document made in Jsoup (the Java html parser) into a string</title> 
    <category scheme="http://stackoverflow.com/tags" term="java" /> 
    <category scheme="http://stackoverflow.com/tags" term="html-parsing" /> 
    <category scheme="http://stackoverflow.com/tags" term="jsoup" />

    <author> 
     <name>
      Hudson Hughes
     </name> 
     <uri>

     </uri> 
    </author> 
    <link rel="alternate" href="http://stackoverflow.com/questions/6865090/how-do-i-convert-a-document-made-in-jsoup-the-java-html-parser-into-a-string"> 
    <published>
     2011-07-28T20:13:55Z
    </published> 
    <updated>
     2015-03-05T11:51:00Z
    </updated> 
    <summary type="html"> &lt;p&gt;I have a document that was made in jsoup that looks like this&lt;/p&gt; &lt;pre&gt;&lt;code&gt;Document doc = Jsoup.connect("http://en.wikipedia.org/").get(); &lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt; &lt;p&gt;How do i convert that &lt;code&gt;doc&lt;/code&gt; into a string.&lt;/p&gt; </summary> 
   </entry> 
   <entry> 
    <id>
     http://stackoverflow.com/questions/6865090/-/6865134#6865134
    </id> 
    <re:rank scheme="http://stackoverflow.com">
     11
    </re:rank> 
    <title type="text">Answer by das_weezul for How do I convert a document made in Jsoup (the Java html parser) into a string</title> 
    <author> 
     <name>
      das_weezul
     </name> 
     <uri>
      http://stackoverflow.com/users/300732
     </uri> 
    </author> 
    <link rel="alternate" href="http://stackoverflow.com/questions/6865090/how-do-i-convert-a-document-made-in-jsoup-the-java-html-parser-into-a-string/6865134#6865134"> 
    <published>
     2011-07-28T20:17:59Z
    </published> 
    <updated>
     2011-07-28T20:31:36Z
    </updated> 
    <summary type="html">&lt;p&gt;Have you tried:&lt;/p&gt; &lt;pre&gt;&lt;code&gt;Document doc = Jsoup.connect("http://en.wikipedia.org/").get(); String htmlString = doc.toString(); &lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt; &lt;p&gt;As &lt;em&gt;Document&lt;/em&gt; extends &lt;em&gt;Element&lt;/em&gt; it also has got the method &lt;em&gt;html()&lt;/em&gt; which "Retrieves the element's inner HTML" according to the &lt;a href="http://jsoup.org/apidocs/"&gt;API&lt;/a&gt;. So that should work:&lt;/p&gt; &lt;pre&gt;&lt;code&gt;Document doc = Jsoup.connect("http://en.wikipedia.org/").get(); String htmlString = doc.html(); &lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Additional Info:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Each &lt;em&gt;Document&lt;/em&gt; object has got a reference to an instance of the inner class &lt;em&gt;Document.OutputSettings&lt;/em&gt; which can be accessed via the method &lt;em&gt;outputSettings()&lt;/em&gt; of Document. There you can enable/disable pretty-printing by using the setter &lt;em&gt;prettyPrint(true/false)&lt;/em&gt;. See the API for &lt;em&gt;Document&lt;/em&gt; and &lt;em&gt;Document.OutputSettings&lt;/em&gt; for furtherinformation&lt;/p&gt; </summary> 
   </entry> 
   <entry> 
    <id>
     http://stackoverflow.com/questions/6865090/-/6865169#6865169
    </id>

    <summary type="html">&lt;p&gt;&lt;code&gt;doc.toString()&lt;/code&gt; works, as does &lt;code&gt;doc.outerHtml()&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt; </summary> 
   </entry>

    <author>

     </name> 
     <uri>

     </uri> 
    </author> 
    <link rel="alternate" href="http://stackoverflow.com/questions/6865090/how-do-i-convert-a-document-made-in-jsoup-the-java-html-parser-into-a-string/25635651#25635651"> 
    <published>
     2014-09-03T03:10:47Z
    </published> 
    <updated>
     2014-09-03T03:10:47Z
    </updated> 
    <summary type="html">&lt;ol&gt; &lt;li&gt;Elements post = d.select("div.post-content");&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;String dd = post.toString();&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Document ddd = Jsoup.parse(dd);&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ol&gt; &lt;p&gt;After parsing the string to document then you can use on it document functions&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ol&gt; &lt;li&gt;Elements scriptTag = ddd.getElementsByTag("script");&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;System.out.println(scriptTag);&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ol&gt; </summary>

      <h2>Stack Exchange Network Terms of Service</h2> 
     </div> 
     <div class="sectionbody"> 
      <div class="sectionbody-full"> 
       <h3>A Note from the Team</h3> 
       <p>The Stack Exchange Network is the easiest way to get expert answers to your questions. We created it to give everyone a chance to be recognized by their peers: recognized for their knowledge, their passion, and their willingness to help others get better at the things they are passionate about. We do ask that you treat our service and community with respect. Spam, personal attacks, and abusive language do not have a place on the Stack Exchange Network. If you ever stumble across anything on the Stack Exchange Network that looks like it violates our policies, please be sure to <a title="Send e-mail to the Stack Exchange team" href="mailto:team@stackexchange.com">let us know</a>.</p> 
       <h3>Accepting the Terms of Service</h3> 
       <p>The Stack Exchange Network (the “Network”) is a set of related Internet sites and other applications for questions and answers, owned and operated by Stack Exchange Inc. (“Stack Exchange”), a Delaware corporation. Please read these terms of service (“Agreement”) carefully before using the Network or any services provided on the Network (collectively, “Services”). By using or accessing the Services, you agree to become bound by all the terms and conditions of this Agreement. If you do not agree to all the terms and conditions of this Agreement, do not use the Services. The Services are accessed by You (“Subscriber” or “You”) under the following terms and conditions:</p> 
       <h3>1. Access to the Services</h3> 
       <p>Subject to the terms and conditions of this Agreement, Stack Exchange may offer to provide the Services, as described more fully on the Network, and which are selected by Subscriber, solely for Subscriber’s own use, and not for the use or benefit of any third party. Services shall include, but not be limited to, any services Stack Exchange performs for Subscriber, as well as the offering of any Content (as defined below) on the Network. Stack Exchange may change, suspend or discontinue the Services at any time, including the availability of any feature, database, or Content. Stack Exchange may also impose limits on certain features and services or restrict Subscriber’s access to parts or all of the Services without notice or liability. Stack Exchange reserves the right, at its discretion, to modify these Terms of Service at any time by posting revised Terms of Service on the Network and by providing notice via e-mail, where possible, or on the Network. Subscriber shall be responsible for reviewing and becoming familiar with any such modifications. Use of the Services by Subscriber following such modification constitutes Subscriber's acceptance of the terms and conditions of this Agreement as modified.</p> 
       <p>Subscriber certifies to Stack Exchange that Subscriber is an individual (i.e., not a corporate entity) at least 13 years of age. No one under the age of 13 may provide any personal information to or on Stack Exchange (including, for example, a name, address, telephone number or email address). Subscriber also certifies that they are legally permitted to use the Services and access the Network, and takes full responsibility for the selection and use of the Services and access of the Network.        <h3>15. Copyright Policy</h3> 
       <p>Stack Exchange has adopted the following policy toward copyright infringement with respect to the Network in accordance with the <a href="http://www.loc.gov/copyright/legislation/dmca.pdf">Digital Millennium Copyright Act</a>. The address of Stack Exchange's Designated Agent for copyright takedown notices (“Designated Agent”) is listed below.</p> 
       <h3>Reporting Copyright Infringements</h3> 
       <p>If You believe that content residing or accessible on the Network infringes a copyright, please send a notice of copyright infringement containing the following information to the Designated Agent at the address below (all received notices will be posted in full to <a href="http://chillingeffects.org">Chilling Effects Clearinghouse</a>):</p> 
       <ol> 
        <li>Identification of the work or material being infringed.</li> 
        <li>Identification of the material that is claimed to be infringing, including its location, with sufficient detail so that Stack Exchange is capable of finding and verifying its existence.</li> 
        <li>Contact information about the notifying party (the Notifying Party), including name, address, telephone number and e-mail address.</li> 
        <li>A statement that the Notifying Party has a good faith belief that the material is not authorized by the copyright owner, its agent or law.</li> 
        <li>A statement made under penalty of perjury that the information provided in the notice is accurate and that the Notifying Party is authorized to make the complaint on behalf of the copyright owner.</li> 
        <li>The Notifying Party's physical or electronic signature.</li> 
       </ol> After the Designated Agent receives notification of an alleged infringement that meets all of the requirements above, Stack Exchange shall: 
       <ol> 
        <li>Disable access to or remove material that it has a reasonable, good faith belief is copyrighted material that has been illegally copied and distributed by any subscriber to the Network.</li> 
        <li>Stack Exchange will then immediately notify the subscriber responsible for the allegedly infringing material (the Offending Subscriber) that it has removed or disabled access to the material.</li> 
        <li>Stack Exchange reserves the right, at its discretion, to immediately terminate the account of any subscriber who is the subject of repeated takedown notices.</li> 
       </ol> 
       <h3>Filing Copyright Counterclaims</h3> 
       <p> A subscriber who believes they are the wrongful subject of a copyright takedown notice may file a counter notification with Stack Exchange by providing the following items in writing to the Designated Agent at the address below (all received notices will be posted in full to <a href="http://chillingeffects.org">Chilling Effects Clearinghouse</a>): </p> 
       <ul> 
        <li>The specific URLs of material that Stack Exchange has removed or to which Stack Exchange has disabled access.</li> 
        <li>User’s name, address, telephone number, and email address.</li> 
        <li>A statement that User consent to the jurisdiction of Federal District Court for the judicial district in which your address is located (or New York County, New York if your address is outside of the United States), and that User will accept service of process from the person who provided notification under subsection (c)(1)(C) or an agent of such person.</li> 
        <li>The following statement: "I swear, under penalty of perjury, that I have a good faith belief that the material was removed or disabled as a result of a mistake or misidentification of the material to be removed or disabled."</li> 
        <li>User’s signature.</li> 
       </ul> 
       <p>Upon receipt of a counterclaim, Stack Exchange will forward it to the party who submitted the original copyright infringement claim. The original complainant will then have 10 days to notify us that he or she has filed legal action relating to the allegedly infringing material. If Stack Exchange does not receive any such notification within 10 days, we may restore the material to the Network.</p> 
       <a name="designatedagent"></a>

      <h1>Tagged Questions</h1> 
      <div id="tabs"> 
       <a href="/tags/hardlink/info" title="information about this tag">info</a> 
       <a class="youarehere" href="/questions/tagged/hardlink?sort=newest&amp;pageSize=50" title="The most recently asked questions">newest</a> 
       <a href="/questions/tagged/hardlink?sort=frequent&amp;pageSize=50" title="Questions with the most links">frequent</a> 
       <a href="/questions/tagged/hardlink?sort=votes&amp;pageSize=50" title="Questions with the most votes">votes</a> 
       <a href="/questions/tagged/hardlink?sort=active&amp;pageSize=50" title="Questions that have recent activity">active</a> 
       <a href="/questions/tagged/hardlink?sort=unanswered&amp;pageSize=50" title="Questions that have no upvoted answers">unanswered</a> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="question"> 
      <div class="welovestackoverflow" style="margin-top: 10px;"> 
       <div style="float: left; position: relative; width: 100%"> 
        <p> A hard link is a directory entry that associates a name with a file or directory on the file-system, in effect creating an alias that may reside elsewhere on the file-system. </p> 
        <p style="margin-bottom: 0;"> <a title="tag wiki" href="/tags/hardlink/info">learn more…</a> <span class="lsep">|</span> <a title="top answerers and askers in this tag" href="/tags/hardlink/topusers">top users</a> <span class="lsep">|</span> <a title="common, alternate spellings or phrasings for this tag" href="/tags/hardlink/synonyms">synonyms</a> </p> 
       </div> 
      </div>

  <title>java - Can't connect Tomcat 6 and oracle 10g XE for jsp database connectivity - Stack Overflow</title> 
  <link rel="shortcut icon" href="//cdn.sstatic.net/stackoverflow/img/favicon.ico?v=6cd6089ee7f6">

  <meta name="twitter:card" content="summary"> 
  <meta name="twitter:domain" content="stackoverflow.com"> 
  <meta property="og:type" content="website"> 
  <meta property="og:image" itemprop="image primaryImageOfPage" content="http://cdn.sstatic.net/stackoverflow/img/apple-touch-icon@2.png?v=ea71a5211a91&amp;a"> 
  <meta name="twitter:title" property="og:title" itemprop="title name" content="Can't connect Tomcat 6 and oracle 10g XE for jsp database connectivity">

            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>I am using Eclispe ganymede,tomcat6 and oracle 10g XE. I have connected all of them.Everything is working fine. </p> 
             <p>But I have created a jsp file which creates a table in database that is not working. There is no error. But when I check into database there is no table created. </p> 
             <p>My coding :</p> 
             <pre><code>    &lt;%@ page language="java" contentType="text/html; charset=ISO-8859-1" pageEncoding="ISO-8859-1"%&gt;
    &lt;!DOCTYPE html PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/loose.dtd"&gt;
    &lt;html&gt;
    &lt;head&gt;
    &lt;meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html; charset=ISO-8859-1"&gt;
    &lt;title&gt;Insert title here&lt;/title&gt;
    &lt;/head&gt;
    &lt;body&gt;
    &lt;%@page import="java.sql.*" %&gt;
    &lt;%
    Connection con=null;
      try
    {
                Class.forName("oracle.jdbc.driver.OracleDriver");
        con=DriverManager.getConnection("jdbc:oracle:thin:@localhost:1521:XE","system","123");
        Statement stmt=con.createStatement();
        stmt.executeUpdate("create table Black ( "
                  + "   id INT PRIMARY KEY, firstName VARCHAR(20), lastName VARCHAR(20), "
                  + "   title VARCHAR(20), salary INT " + ")");
        out.println("Table Created");

    }
    catch(ClassNotFoundException e)
    {
        out.println(e.getMessage());
    }
    catch(NamingException e)
    {
    out.println(e.getMessage());    
    }
    finally
    {
        try
        {

            if(con!=null)
                con.close();

        }
        catch(SQLException e)
        {
        }
    }
    %&gt;

    &lt;/body&gt;
    &lt;/html&gt;
</code></pre>

       <a name="7056737"></a> 
       <div id="answer-7056737" class="answer" data-answerid="7056737" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer"> 
        <table> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td class="votecell"> 
            <div class="vote"> 
             <input type="hidden" name="_id_" value="7056737"> 
             <a class="vote-up-off" title="This answer is useful">up vote</a> 
             <span itemprop="upvoteCount" class="vote-count-post ">2</span> 
             <a class="vote-down-off" title="This answer is not useful">down vote</a> 
            </div> </td> 
           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>What is the output, is there a stacktrace? Have you defined the datasource as testdb?</p> 
             <p>You shouldnt anyway be doing sql-statements from a JSP page, put the sql-statements behind a DAO or use Hibernate or similar ORM tool. </p> 
             <p>Here is the <a href="http://www.oracle.com/technetwork/database/features/jdbc/index-091264.html" rel="nofollow">http://www.oracle.com/technetwork/database/features/jdbc/index-091264.html</a> download page for Oracles JDBC drivers. Take the matching one for your database, and the matching version of your Java vm. And put it under your tomcats lib/ directory.</p> 
            </div>

           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>Any exceptions raised ?. Don't use JDBC connection code in Jsp .Instead keep in a DAO class.</p> 
             <p>Or Jsp tab libraries can be used.</p> 
             <p><a href="http://download.oracle.com/javaee/1.4/tutorial/doc/JSTL7.html" rel="nofollow">SQL Tag Library</a></p> 
             <p>Check this link to solve the issue .</p> 
             <p><a href="http://www.coderanch.com/t/303703/JDBC/java/Oracle-jdbc-driver-OracleDriver" rel="nofollow">Oracle.jdbc. driver.OracleDriver problem</a></p> 
            </div>

       <div id="answer-8804668" class="answer" data-answerid="8804668" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer"> 
        <table> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td class="votecell"> 
            <div class="vote"> 
             <input type="hidden" name="_id_" value="8804668"> 
             <a class="vote-up-off" title="This answer is useful">up vote</a> 
             <span itemprop="upvoteCount" class="vote-count-post ">1</span> 
             <a class="vote-down-off" title="This answer is not useful">down vote</a> 
            </div> </td> 
           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>You need to include the ojdbc14.jar file in your Deployment Assembly in your project. Using eclipse :</p> 
             <p><strong>proj --&gt; properties --&gt; Deployment Assembly --&gt; Add --&gt; Add your jar file.</strong></p> 
            </div>

             <a class="vote-down-off" title="This answer is not useful">down vote</a> 
            </div> </td> 
           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>I want to add that in my project I had to change from:</p> 
             <pre><code>String driverName = "oracle.jdbc.driver.OracleDriver";
</code></pre> 
             <p>to</p> 
             <pre><code>String driverName = "oracle.jdbc.OracleDriver";
</code></pre> 
             <p>I am using Oracle Database 11g Release 2.</p> 
            </div>

        <div class="subheader answers-subheader"> 
         <h2> 1 Answer <span style="display:none;" itemprop="answerCount">1</span> </h2> 
         <div> 
          <div id="tabs"> 
           <a href="/questions/85862/why-did-greedo-shoot-first?answertab=active#tab-top" title="Answers with the latest activity first">active</a> 
           <a href="/questions/85862/why-did-greedo-shoot-first?answertab=oldest#tab-top" title="Answers in the order they were provided">oldest</a> 
           <a class="youarehere" href="/questions/85862/why-did-greedo-shoot-first?answertab=votes#tab-top" title="Answers with the highest score first">votes</a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <a name="85864"></a> 
       <div id="answer-85864" class="answer" data-answerid="85864" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Answer"> 
        <table> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td class="votecell"> 
            <div class="vote"> 
             <input type="hidden" name="_id_" value="85864"> 
             <a class="vote-up-off" title="This answer is useful">up vote</a> 
             <span itemprop="upvoteCount" class="vote-count-post ">33</span> 
             <a class="vote-down-off" title="This answer is not useful">down vote</a> 
            </div> </td> 
           <td class="answercell"> 
            <div class="post-text" itemprop="text"> 
             <p>Yes, Lucas addressed this controversy in <a href="http://www.hollywoodreporter.com/heat-vision/george-lucas-star-wars-interview-288523">an interview with <em>The Hollywood Reporter</em></a> in 2012:</p> 
             <blockquote> 
              <p><strong>Lucas:</strong> The controversy over who shot first, Greedo or Han Solo, in <em>Episode IV</em>, what I did was try to clean up the confusion, but obviously it upset people because they wanted Solo [who seemed to be the one who shot first in the original] to be a cold-blooded killer, but he actually isn't. It had been done in all close-ups and it was confusing about who did what to whom. I put a little wider shot in there that made it clear that Greedo is the one who shot first, but everyone wanted to think that Han shot first, because they wanted to think that he actually just gunned him down.</p> 
             </blockquote> 
             <p>He goes on to compare this change to replacing the puppet Yoda in <em>Phantom Menace</em> with CGI, as was done in the later films. Ultimately, this is an example of Lucas using CGI to make older films more true to his creative vision; in Lucas' mind, Greedo <em>always</em> shot first.</p> 
             <p>Interesting, this is contradicted by <a href="http://www.imsdb.com/scripts/Star-Wars-A-New-Hope.html">the script</a>:</p> 
             <blockquote> 
              <p><strong>Greedo</strong> I've been looking forward to killing you for a long time.</p> 
              <p><strong>Han:</strong> I bet you have.</p> 
              <p>Suddenly the slimy alien disappears in a blinding flash of light. Han pulls his smoking gun from beneath the table as the other patron look on in bemused amazement. Han gets up and starts out of the cantina, flipping the bartender some coins as he leaves.</p> 
             </blockquote> 
             <p>The novelization (which, despite having Lucas' name on the cover, was actually written by Alan Dean Foster but presumably <em>approved</em> by Lucas) also contradicts Lucas' statement:</p> 
             <blockquote> 
              <p>"Over my dead body," Solo said unamiably.</p> 
              <p>[Greedo] was not impressed. "If you insist. Will you come outside with me, or must I finish it here?"</p> 
              <p>"I don't think they'd like another killing in here," Solo pointed out.</p> 
              <p>Something which might have been a laugh came from the creature's translator. "They'd hardly notice. Get up, Solo. I've been looking forward to this for a long time. You've embarrassed me in front of Jabba for the last time."</p> 
              <p>"I think you're right."</p> 
              <p>Light and noise filled the little corner of the cantina, and when it had faded, all that remained of the unctuous alien was a smoking, slimy spot on the stone floor.</p> 
              <p>Solo brought his hand to the smoking weapon it held out from beneath the table, drawing bemused stares from several of the cantina's patrons and clucking sounds from its more knowledgeable ones. They had known the creature had committed its fatal mistake in allowing Solo the chance to get his hands under cover.</p> 
              <p><sup><sub><em>Star Wars</em> (novelization) Chapter 7</sub></sup></p> 
             </blockquote> 
             <p>No mention is made of Greedo shooting <em>at all</em>. Chalk it up to Lucas' historical revisionism, I guess.</p> 
             <p>However, as <a href="https://scifi.stackexchange.com/questions/85862/why-did-greedo-shoot-first#comment187376_85864">phantom42 notes in comments</a>, they've been slowly rectifying this over the years:</p> 
             <ul> 
              <li><p>The initial controversy came from the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_changes_in_Star_Wars_re-releases#1997_Star_Wars_Trilogy_Special_Edition">1997 Special Edition release</a></p></li> 
              <li><p>In the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_changes_in_Star_Wars_re-releases#Episode_IV:_A_New_Hope_3">2004 DVD release</a>, the timing is shortened slightly; Greedo fires first, but only just. <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fKxOEUhRMt0">A diligent YouTuber compares the 2004 scene to the 1997</a>:</p> <p> </p>
               <div style="z-index:0;"> 
                <object style="height: 385px; width: 640px"> <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/fKxOEUhRMt0?version=3&amp;start=0&amp;feature=player_embedded"> <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true"> <param name="allowScriptAccess" value="always"> <param name="wmode" value="opaque"> <embed src="http://www.youtube.com/v/fKxOEUhRMt0?version=3&amp;start=0&amp;feature=player_embedded" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" allowfullscreen="true" allowscriptaccess="always" width="640" height="385" wmode="transparent"> </object> 
               </div><p></p></li> 
              <li><p>In the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_changes_in_Star_Wars_re-releases#Episode_IV:_A_New_Hope_4">2011 Blu-Ray release</a>, it's shortened again; Han and Greedo now shoot at basically the exact same time. <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=v-xdepfah98">The 2011 scene is also on YouTube</a>:</p> <p> </p>
               <div style="z-index:0;"> 
                <object style="height: 385px; width: 640px"> <param name="movie" value="http://www.youtube.com/v/v-xdepfah98?version=3&amp;start=0&amp;feature=player_embedded"> <param name="allowFullScreen" value="true"> <param name="allowScriptAccess" value="always"> <param name="wmode" value="opaque"> <embed src="http://www.youtube.com/v/v-xdepfah98?version=3&amp;start=0&amp;feature=player_embedded" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" allowfullscreen="true" allowscriptaccess="always" width="640" height="385" wmode="transparent"> </object> 
               </div><p></p></li> 
             </ul> 
            </div>
